soup = BeautifulSoup(html_doc, 'html.parser')

# Extract title

chapter_title = title_tag.get_text(strip=True) if title_tag else "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y tiÃªu Ä‘á» chÆ°Æ¡ng"

# Extract main content
content_tags = soup.find_all('p', id=lambda x: x and (x.startswith('L') or x.startswith('La')))

# Function to process ruby tags
def process_ruby(tag):
    rt_text = tag.find('rt')
    rp_text_open = tag.find('rp', string='(')
    rp_text_close = tag.find('rp', string=')')
    
    main_text = ''.join(tag.find_all(string=True, recursive=False)).strip() # Get text directly under ruby tag
    
    if rp_text_open and rp_text_close and rt_text:
        # Check for specific ruby usage for names/terms that should be kept as is or translated with furigana
        # For example, ã€Œã‚µãƒ³ãƒ©ã‚¯ã€ would be in furigana. The original text is å…ˆé ­.
        # So we want `main_text (rt_text.text)`
        
        # Specific handling for the "..." furigana indicating hidden meaning
        if rt_text.text == 'ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»':
            if main_text == 'åŠ©å¤ªåˆ€':
                return 'sá»± trá»£ giÃºp'
            # Add more cases if needed for '...'
        elif rt_text.text == 'ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»':
            if main_text == 'æˆ¦ã‚ã•ã‚ŒãŸ':
                return 'bá»‹ buá»™c pháº£i chiáº¿n Ä‘áº¥u'
            if main_text == 'é§†ã‘è½ã¡ã‚‹':
                return 'lao xuá»‘ng'
        elif rt_text.text == 'ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»ãƒ»':
            if main_text == 'ç¥€ã‚‰ã‚Œã—ã‚‚ã®':
                return 'thá»© Ä‘Æ°á»£c thá» phá»¥ng'
        
        # Handle special characters in rt_text for quotes
        if 'ã€Œ' in rt_text.text and 'ã€' in rt_text.text:
            rt_clean = rt_text.text.replace('ã€Œ', 'â€œ').replace('ã€', 'â€')
            return f"{main_text} ({rt_clean})"
        
        # Handle ã€Šã€‹ for official names
        parent_text = tag.parent.get_text() # Get text of parent to see if ã€Šã€‹ is present
        if 'ã€Š' in parent_text and 'ã€‹' in parent_text:
             return f"{main_text} ({rt_text.text})" # Keep both
        
        # Standard ruby (main_text + furigana)
        return f"{main_text} ({rt_text.text})"
    return main_text # Fallback if ruby structure is not as expected

translated_content = []

# Add chapter title
translated_content.append(chapter_title.upper())

for p_tag in content_tags:
    # Process ruby tags within each paragraph
    ruby_tags = p_tag.find_all('ruby')
    for ruby_tag in ruby_tags:
        processed_text = process_ruby(ruby_tag)
        ruby_tag.replace_with(processed_text)
    
    paragraph_text = p_tag.get_text(strip=True)
    
    # Replace Japanese quotation marks with Vietnamese ones for dialogue
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('ã€Œ', 'â€œ').replace('ã€', 'â€')
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('ã€', 'â€œ').replace('ã€', 'â€') # Assuming ã€ã€ is also dialogue or needs to be converted

    # Specific Japanese punctuation conversions
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('â€¦â€¦', 'â€¦') # Often used as ellipsis
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('ã€', ', ') # Comma
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('ã€‚', '.') # Period
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('ï¼', '!') # Exclamation
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('ï¼Ÿ', '?') # Question mark
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('ï¼š', ': ') # Colon
    paragraph_text = paragraph_text.replace('â”€', 'â€”') # Em dash

    # Additional cleanup for multiple spaces
    paragraph_text = ' '.join(paragraph_text.split())

    if paragraph_text:
        translated_content.append(paragraph_text)
